    // 计算结果提交
    function cityJsqSubmit() {
        var cityid = $("#navCity  option:selected").val();
        var housearea = $("#housearea").val();
        var shi = $("#shiselect  option:selected").val();
        var chu = $("#chuselect  option:selected").val();
        var wei = $("#weiselect  option:selected").val();
        var ting = $("#tingselect  option:selected").val();
        var yt = $("#ytselect  option:selected").val();
        var phone = $("#phone1").val();
        var name = $("#name1").val();
        if (isEmpty(cityid)) {
            alert("请选择城市");
            return;
        }
        if (!isNumber(housearea) && !isDecimal(housearea)) {
            alert("房屋面积必须是数字或者包含两位小数");
            return;
        }
        if (!isMoblie(phone)) {
            alert("请输入正确的手机号码");
            return;
        }
        if (isEmpty(name)) {
            alert("你的姓名必须填写");
            return;
        }
        if (!isApplySubmit) {
            alert("请勿重复提交或者请刷新页面重试！");
            return;
        } else if (!slideVerifyVal4) {
            alert("请滑动滑块通过验证");
            return;
        } else {
            var remark = "所在城市：" + $("#navCity  option:selected").text() + " 建筑面积：" + housearea + " 装修档次：";
            $("#remark").val(remark);
            isApplySubmit = false;
            var alertStr = "保驾护航装修网温馨提示：\n*本价格为毛坯房半包估算价格(不含水电报价)，实际装修报价以量房实测为准。\n*您的信息将被严格保密！稍后客服人员将以客服总机0592电话与您取得联系，请保持电话畅通。"
            saveactivity("cityJsqForm", phone, "", false, alertStr);
            decorationBudgetNew(cityid, housearea, shi, chu, wei, false, ting, yt);
            setTimeout(function () {
                isApplySubmit = true;
            }, 3000);
            slideVerify4.resetVerify();
            slideVerifyVal4 = false
        }
    }

    function setJsqSpan(arr) {
        var html = "";
        for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
            html += "<span>" + arr[i] + "</span>";
        }
        return html;
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function () {
        // 头部城市定位
        var areaName = getCookie("areaName");
        if (isEmpty(areaName)) {
            $("#headerAreaName").text("厦门");
        } else {
            var ch = '"';
            var areaNameTemp = decodeURIComponent(areaName).replace("市", '').replace(new RegExp(ch, 'g'), '');
            $("#headerAreaName").text(areaNameTemp);
        }
        // 装企宝登录身份地址判断
        var $headerUsername = $("#headerUsername");
        var $headerManagementCenter = $("#headerManagementCenter");
        var $headerLogout = $("#headerLogout");
        var $headerLogin = $("#headerLogin");
        var $headerRegister = $("#headerRegister");
        var $baoLogin = $("#baoLogin");
        var $baoNotLogining = $("#baoNotLogining");
        // 判断登录角色
        var centerHtml = "";
        var personBusinessDesigner = getCookie("personBusinessDesigner");
        if (personBusinessDesigner != null && personBusinessDesigner == "business") {
            centerHtml = "<a href='http://www.bao315.com/business/baoMain.html' target='_blank'>[商家中心]</a>";
        } else if (personBusinessDesigner != null && personBusinessDesigner == "designer") {
            centerHtml = "<a href='http://www.bao315.com/designer_center/main.html' target='_blank'>[设计师中心]</a>";
        } else {
            centerHtml = "<a href='http://www.bao315.com/member/main.html' target='_blank'>[个人中心]</a>";
        }
        // 判断装企宝地址
        var baoUrl = "http://testbao.bao315.com";
        var href = window.location.href;
        if (href.indexOf("test") < 0) {
            baoUrl = "http://bao.bao315.com";
        }
        var baoLoginHtml = "<a href='" + baoUrl + "' target='_blank'>装企宝SaaS</a>";
        var baoNoLoginHtml = "<a href='" + baoUrl + "'>装企宝SaaS</a>";
        var name = getCookie("username");
        if (isEmpty(name)) {
            $headerUsername.text("").hide();
            $headerManagementCenter.html(centerHtml).hide();
            $headerRegister.show();
            $headerLogin.show();
            $headerLogout.hide();
            $baoLogin.html(baoLoginHtml).hide();
            $baoNotLogining.html(baoNoLoginHtml).show();
            $("#loginLine").show();
        } else {
            var ch = '"';
            name = decodeURIComponent(String(name)).replace(new RegExp(ch, 'g'), '');
            $headerUsername.text(name).show();
            $headerManagementCenter.html(centerHtml).show();
            $headerLogout.show();
            $headerRegister.hide();
            $headerLogin.hide();
            $baoLogin.html(baoLoginHtml).show();
            $baoNotLogining.html(baoNoLoginHtml).hide();
            $("#loginLine").hide();
        }
        // 头部导航栏悬浮
        $('.nav-col').hover(function () {
            var index01 = $(this).index();
            $(this).addClass('active01');
            $('.nav-cont-div-zt').hide();
            $('.nav-cont-zt').children().eq(index01).toggle()
        }, function () {
            $(this).removeClass('active01')
        });
        $('.nav-cont-zt').mouseleave(function () {
            $('.nav-cont-zt').children().stop().hide('fast');
        });
        // 导航头部搜索按钮
        $("#searchKey").keydown(function (e) {
            var keyCode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which ? e.which : e.charCode; //兼容IE 火狐 谷歌
            if (keyCode == 13) {
                searchButton();
            }
        });
        // 添加装企宝商家浏览网站记录
        var userId = "";
        $.ajax({
            url: 'http://www.bao315.com/login/getUserId.html',
            type: "get",
            dataType: "jsonp",
            data: {},
            success: function (data) {
                if (data.errcode == 0) {
                    if (data.result) {
                        userId = data.result;
                        // console.log("request getUserId userId:" + userId);
                        $.ajax({
                            url: 'http://www.bao315.com/login/addUserBrowseLog.html',
                            type: "get",
                            dataType: "jsonp",
                            data: {
                                userId: userId
                            },
                            success: function (data) {
                                if (data.errcode == 0) {
                                    // console.log("request addUserBrowseLog userId:" + userId);
                                }
                            }
                        })
                    }
                } else {
                    console.log("request getUserId failure:" + data.errmsg);
                }
            }
        });
    });

    // 搜索按钮事件
    function searchButton() {
        var areaNumber = getCookie("areaNumber");
        var $keyword = $("input[name='searchKey']").val();
        $keyword = $.trim($keyword);
        if ($keyword != null && $keyword.length > 0) {
            var reg = /^(\w|[\u4E00-\u9FA5])*$/;
            if (!$keyword.match(reg)) {
                $.myBox.alert("提示", "您的输入有误，请误输入特殊字符");
                return;
            }
            location.href = "http://xm.bao315.com/companies/searchList/?keyword=" + $keyword;
        }
    }


    function findLocalCity() {
        $.ajax({
            url: "http://www.bao315.com/findLocalCity.html",
            data: {},
            type: "get",
            dataType: "json",
            cache: false,
            success: function (data) {
                if (data != null && data.errcode == 0) {
                    var areaNumber = data.result.areaNumber;
                    var areaName = data.result.areaName;
                    if (areaNumber != null) {
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(4).attr("href", "http://" + areaNumber + ".bao315.com/companies");
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(5).attr("href", "http://" + areaNumber + ".bao315.com/designer");
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(0).attr("href", "http://" + areaNumber + ".bao315.com/");
                    } else {
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(4).attr("href", "http://xm.bao315.com/companies");
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(5).attr("href", "http://xm.bao315.com/designer");
                        $("#nav-main-white").children().eq(0).attr("href", "http://xm.bao315.com/");
                    }
                    if (areaName != null) {
                        var areaNameTemp = areaName.replace("市", '').replace("\"", '').replace("\"", '');
                        if (areaNameTemp != null && areaNameTemp != undefined && areaNameTemp.length > 4) {
                            $('#headerAreaName').addClass("headerAreaName");
                        }
                        $("#headerAreaName").text(areaNameTemp);
                    } else {
                        $("#headerAreaName").text("厦门");
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

<script>
    $().ready(function () {
        //初始化城市导航省市联动
        initProvinceCity2("navProvince_index", null, "navCity_index", null, "http://www.bao315.com/area/area_open.html");

        $("#navCityOpen").click(function () {
            var $areaId = $("#city").val();
            if ($areaId != null && $areaId != undefined && $areaId > 0) {
                $.ajax({
                    url: 'http://www.bao315.com/area/areaInfo.html',
                    type: "GET",
                    data: {cityId: $areaId},
                    dataType: "json",
                    cache: false,
                    async: false,
                    success: function (data) {
                        if ($.isEmptyObject(data)) {
                            return;
                        }
                        if (data["isHot"] == 2 && data["isOpen"] == 1 && data["areaNumber"] != null && data["areaNumber"] != undefined) {
                            location.href = "http://" + data["areaNumber"] + ".bao315.com/";
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $('.left-flex ul li:nth-child(2)').hover(function () {
            $('.qr-code').show();
        }, function () {
            $('.qr-code').hide();
        });
        $('.left-flex ul li:nth-child(1)').hover(function () {
            $('.left-consultation').show();
        }, function () {
            $('.left-consultation').hide();
        });
        $('.left-flex ul li').eq(2).click(function () {
            $("html,body").animate({
                scrollTop: 0
            }, 200);
        });
        $('.index-06-width div').hover(function () {
            index = $(this).index();
            $(this).children('p').stop().slideDown();
        }, function () {
            $(this).children('p').stop().slideUp();
        });
        //tab切换
        $("#score").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").show();
            $("#hotlist").hide();
            $("#signinglist").hide();
            $("#score").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#score').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        $("#hot").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").hide();
            $("#hotlist").show();
            $("#signinglist").hide();
            $("#hot").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#hot').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        $("#signing").click(function () {
            $("#scorelist").hide();
            $("#hotlist").hide();
            $("#signinglist").show();
            $("#signing").css({
                "background": '#de0010',
                "color": '#fff'
            });
            $('#signing').siblings().css({
                "background": '#fff',
                "color": '#666'
            });
        });
        //tab切换结束
        $('body').on('click', '.province-sele-option p', function () {
            $('#province').val($(this).attr('id')).change();
            $('#navCity1').html("选择城市");

        });
        $('body').on('click', '.city-sele-option-01 p', function () {
            $('#city').val($(this).attr('id')).change();

        });
        $('.city-list .wrap-a a').each((i, v) => {
            if ($(v).text().length > 4) {
                $(v).css({
                    'width': 'auto',
                    'margin-right': '40px'
                })
            } else {
                $(v).css('width', '120px')
            }
        })
    });
</script>
